## ğŸ¯ Tutorial Overview

This comprehensive tutorial covers **every single feature** in Pj Buddy with:
- **Precise UI highlighting** (exact elements to focus on)

**How to Use**: Follow each step sequentially, or jump to specific features using the table of contents.

**ğŸ“ Manual Instructions**:
1. Enter your **Business Name**
2. Select your **Location** (city/suburb)

6. Set **Work Hours** (Monday-Friday 8am-6pm)
7. Enable/Disable **Emergency Service**
8. Click "Complete Setup"

### ğŸš€ Quick Start Commands

**Most Common Chat Commands:**
```
"New job for John, bathroom reno, $8500"
"Show my schedule for tomorrow"
"Find contact Jane Smith"
"Create quote for deck build 4x6 meters"
"What's my revenue this month?"
"Call John Smith"
```

**Magic Commands:**
- `/draft` - Create new deal
- `/summarize` - Get overview  
- `/schedule` - Check availability
- `/quote` - Generate quote
- `/email` - Draft email
